If there are clusters of apples that are far from players, it might be beneficial to vote for a move that brings us closer to those clusters. This would allow us to harvest more apples in the long run, as apples grow faster when there are more apples nearby.\n\nSecondly, I would consider the actions of the other players. If they are acting competitively and trying to hoard apples for themselves, it might be more beneficial to vote for a move that allows me to collect apples independently. However, if they are acting cooperatively and are willing to share the apples, it might be more beneficial to vote for a move that brings us closer together.
